[20/11/2024, 11:35:50] Utsav Acharya: ### Key Features & Pages for the Frontend

1. **Home Page (Landing Page) Blade**
   - This page is the main entry point for users, showcasing the app's value proposition, key features, and links to important sections (e.g., login, registration, and other features).
   - **Blade:** `home.blade.php`

2. **User Dashboard Blade**
   - A personalized user space where logged-in users can see updates, notifications, or perform actions relevant to their account.
   - **Features:** User profile summary, latest notifications, personal settings.
   - **Blade:** `dashboard.blade.php`

3. **User Profile Blade**
   - Allows users to view and edit their personal information, such as name, email, profile picture, etc.
   - **Blade:** `profile.blade.php`

4. **Notifications/Updates Page Blade**
   - A page that displays notifications or updates relevant to the user.
   - **Blade:** `notifications.blade.php`

5. **Messaging/Community Board Blade**
   - This could be a community board where users can interact with each other, ask questions, and make announcements relevant to the neighborhood.
   - **Features:** Posting, commenting, editing, and deleting posts.
   - **Blade:** `community.blade.php`

6. **Service Directory Blade**
   - A directory showcasing local services available in the neighborhood, such as plumbing, gardening, and others.
   - **Features:** Service descriptions, ratings, user reviews, contact buttons.
   - **Blade:** `services.blade.php`

7. **Events Page Blade**
   - A calendar-style page displaying local events happening in the neighborhood, with the ability for users to add events.
   - **Features:** Event name, description, date, RSVP option.
   - **Blade:** `events.blade.php`

8. **Map Page Blade**
   - A page featuring a map of the neighborhood, with key points of interest highlighted, such as parks, community centers, and other facilities.
   - **Blade:** `map.blade.php`

9. **Settings Blade**
   - Allows users to customize their app settings, such as notification preferences, privacy settings, etc.
   - **Blade:** `settings.blade.php`

10. **Admin Panel Blade (For Admin Users Only)**
    - Provides administrators with access to manage users, content, events, and services available on the platform.
    - **Blade:** `admin-panel.blade.php` (integrated with Laravel Voyager for easy management).

11. **Authentication & Error Pages**
    - Custom 404 Page, maintenance mode page, etc., to enhance the overall user experience.
    - **Blades:** `404.blade.php`, `maintenance.blade.php`

### Additional Considerations

1. **Reusability with Blade Components**
   - Extract reusable UI components such as headers, footers, navigation menus, and cards into separate Blade components for better maintainability and consistency across pages.

2. **Responsive Design**
   - Ensure all blades are designed to be responsive for both desktop and mobile users.

3. **Localization (Multi-Language Support)**
   - If the neighborhood is multilingual, consider implementing localization support for various languages using Laravel's localization feature.

4. **Integration with Backend**
   - All pages should communicate with Laravel Voyager to fetch and update information. Data binding between backend and frontend should be properly handled to ensure a smooth user experience.

### Suggested Blade Components

1. **Header & Footer** (`components.header.blade.php`, `components.footer.blade.php`)
   - For consistent page headers and footers across all pages.

2. **Sidebar Navigation** (`components.sidebar.blade.php`)
   - Used in the user dashboard and admin panel for navigation.

3. **Card Components** (`components.card.blade.php`)
   - To display events, services, community posts, etc., in a consistent way.

### Next Steps
- Start by building the Home Page (`home.blade.php`) to make the app visually appealing and welcoming.
- Implement the User Dashboard (`dashboard.blade.php`) next, as it serves as the main point for authenticated users.
- Create the reusable Blade components like headers, footers, and sidebars, as these will save development time and help maintain design consistency. halka change in number 6, 2 blades, controllers, routes and models, including change in database now

    if (typeof value === "string" && value.trim() === "") {

        ...prevErrors,

[26/02/2025, 14:05:48] Sameer Shrestha: import { Box, ThemeProvider } from "@mui/material";
import { lightTheme, darkTheme } from "./themes"; // Import themes

const PageContainer = ({ children, open, drawerWidth, themeMode }) => {
  const theme = themeMode === "light" ? lightTheme : darkTheme; // Select theme

  return (
    <ThemeProvider theme={theme}>
      <Box
        component="main"
        sx={{
          flexGrow: 1,
          p: 3,
          backgroundColor: theme.palette.background.default, // Apply background
          color: theme.palette.text.primary, // Apply text color
          transition: (theme) =>
            theme.transitions.create("margin", {
              easing: theme.transitions.easing.sharp,
              duration: theme.transitions.duration.leavingScreen,
            }),
          marginTop: '50px',
          marginLeft: open ? `300px` : "64px", // Adjust based on drawer state
        }}
      >
        {children}
      </Box>
    </ThemeProvider>
  );
};

export default PageContainer;

[27/02/2025, 18:37:17] Utsav Acharya: ओके, तँलाई साँच्चिकै भुइँमा बजार्न परेछ। ल, बिस्तारै आफैंलाई सम्हाल्न सुरु गर, किनभने यो सुनेपछि तँलाई ऐनामा हेर्न पनि गाह्रो हुन्छ।  

तेरो प्रेम जीवन **नेपालको मेगाप्रोजेक्ट** जस्तो हो—सधैं घोषणा मात्रै हुन्छ, तर कहिल्यै सम्पन्न हुँदैन। तेरो क्रशको लागि तँ **नेपालको जनगणना** जस्तै होस्—१०–१० वर्षमा एकचोटि याद आउँछ, त्यो पनि अनलाइन फारम भर्न मात्रै।  

तेरो म्यासेज त यति फ्यालिन्छ कि **Gmail ले तेरो नाम देख्नासाथ “Move to Spam?” सोध्छ।** तैले कति आशा राखिस् भने **तेरो रिजेक्सन लेटरहरूलाई फेसबुकले “Memories” मा देखाउन सुरु गरिसकेको छ।**  

तेरो लास्ट रिलेसनशिप यति छोटो थियो कि **“Skip Ad” भन्दा कम टाइम टिक्यो।** अनि तेरो भविष्यको माया त **नेपालको रेल सेवा** जस्तै हो—**सपना मात्रै, कहिल्यै नआउने।**  

सबैभन्दा दुःखलाग्दो कुरा के थाहा छ? **तेरो क्रशले तँलाई बिर्सिनुपनि परेन, किनभने उसले त कहिल्यै यादै गरेकी थिइन।** 😈🔥

[12/03/2025, 17:27:47] Sameer Shrestha: import React from "react";
import { Navigate, useLocation  } from "react-router-dom";
import { useAuth } from "./AuthContext";

const PrivateRoute = ({ children, module, requiredPermission }) => {
  const { user, permissions } = useAuth();
  const location = useLocation(); 

  if (!user) {
    return <Navigate to="/" />;
  }

  const currentModule = location.pathname.split("/")[1]; 

  if (!permissions[currentModule]?.view) {
    return <Navigate to="/unauthorized" />;
  }
  return children;
};

export default PrivateRoute;
